Error

When an error is encountered by a client, it will send diagnositc information to this service which will log the information for later analysis.

/errors post

post

Add a new error to the collection

post /errors

Add a new error to the collection

  • Request
  • Response

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Error",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["errorCode", "message", "url", "logHistory", "version"],
    "properties": {
        "id": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "number"
        },
        "errorCode": {
            "type": "string"
        },
        "message": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "diagnostic error message"
        },
        "url": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "full URL the user was viewing when the error occurred"
        },
        "version": {
            "type": "string",
            "description": "the version of the ui when the error was logged"
        },
        "logHistory": {
            "description": "most recent client-side logging messages",
            "type": "array",
            "items": {
                "type": "string"
            }
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
    "errorCode": "Error",
    "message": "An error occurred",
    "url": "http://www.app.com/#page",
    "version": "foobar",
    "logHistory": [
        "stack trace line 1",
        "stack trace line 2"
    ]
}

HTTP status code 204

The request was successfully handled

HTTP status code 409

Unable to process request to do conflict in state of object

Users

Management of user resources

/users post get

post

Add a new user to the collection

get

Get a list of user

post /users

Add a new user to the collection

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/User",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["email","firstName","lastName","profileImageUrl","roles"],
    "properties": {
        "id": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "number"
        },
        "email": {
            "description": "The user email address",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "firstName": {
            "description": "The users first name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "lastName": {
            "description": "The users last name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "profileImageUrl": {
            "description": "The users profile image URL",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "roles": {
            "description": "The users system roles associated with the user",
            "type": "array",
            "items": {
                "type": "string"
            }
        },
        "address": {
            "description": "The address of this user",
            "$ref": "Address"
        },
        "phone": {
            "description": "The phone number of this user",
            "type": "string"
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
    "id": 1,
    "email": "jdoe@anywhere.com",
    "firstName": "John",
    "lastName": "Doe",
    "profileImageUrl": "assets/temp/John_Smith.jpg",
    "roles": []
}

HTTP status code 201

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/User",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["email","firstName","lastName","profileImageUrl","roles"],
    "properties": {
        "id": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "number"
        },
        "email": {
            "description": "The user email address",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "firstName": {
            "description": "The users first name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "lastName": {
            "description": "The users last name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "profileImageUrl": {
            "description": "The users profile image URL",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "roles": {
            "description": "The users system roles associated with the user",
            "type": "array",
            "items": {
                "type": "string"
            }
        },
        "address": {
            "description": "The address of this user",
            "$ref": "Address"
        },
        "phone": {
            "description": "The phone number of this user",
            "type": "string"
        }

    "email": "jdoe@anywhere.com",

HTTP status code 299

This is a mock service that has not yet been implemented

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 409

Unable to process request to do conflict in state of object. Any specific details included in body.

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those

get /users

Get a list of user

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer - default: 1)

    The page number of the collection to return

    Example:

    ?page=1
  • pageSize: (integer)

    The number of items to display per page

    Example:

    ?pageSize=10
  • sortBy: (string)

    A field to sort the paged collection by

    Example:

    ?sortBy=name
  • sortDescending: (boolean - default: false)

    Sort results in descending order rather than ascending

    Example:

    ?sortDescending=true
  • name: (string)

    Returns any users partially matching given name

    Example:

    ?name=john

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/UserCollection",
    "type": "array",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "items": {
        "$ref": "User"
    }
}

Example:

[
    {
        "id": 1,
        "email": "jdoe@anywhere.com",
        "firstName": "John",
        "lastName": "Doe",
        "profileImageUrl": "assets/temp/John_Smith.jpg",
        "roles": []
    }
]

{
    "id": "http://types/Count",
    "type": "integer",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "description": "The count for an associated collection"
}

Example:

put /users/{id}

Update a specific user

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • id: required (number)

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/User",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["email","firstName","lastName","profileImageUrl","roles"],
    "properties": {
        "id": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "number"
        },
        "email": {
            "description": "The user email address",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "firstName": {
            "description": "The users first name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "lastName": {
            "description": "The users last name",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "profileImageUrl": {
            "description": "The users profile image URL",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "roles": {
            "description": "The users system roles associated with the user",
            "type": "array",
            "items": {
                "type": "string"
            }
        },
        "address": {
            "description": "The address of this user",
            "$ref": "Address"
        },
        "phone": {
            "description": "The phone number of this user",
            "type": "string"
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
    "id": 1,
    "email": "jdoe@anywhere.com",
    "firstName": "John",
    "lastName": "Doe",
    "profileImageUrl": "assets/temp/John_Smith.jpg",
    "roles": []
}

Login

Management of user authorizations

/login post delete put

post

Authenticate the user via email & password

delete

Clears current session and logs user out of the application.

put

Returns an updated token with an extended expiration. This will be invoked by the client when the user has been actively using the client but not in ways that have resulted in a other service calls. It allows the client to prevent the user from being timed out unnecessarily.

post /login

Authenticate the user via email & password

  • Request
  • Response

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Login",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["email"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "email": {
            "description": "The userName of the authenticated user",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "password": {
            "description": "The password of the authenticated user (not returned in response)",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "user": {
            "description": "The authenticated user",
            "$ref": "User"
        },
        "token": {
            "description": "JWT token containing claims for exp, roles, and permissions (not part of request, only response)",
            "type": "string"
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
  "email": "jdoe@somewhere.com",
  "password": "pword"
}

HTTP status code 201

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Login",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["email"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "email": {
            "description": "The userName of the authenticated user",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "password": {
            "description": "The password of the authenticated user (not returned in response)",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "user": {
            "description": "The authenticated user",
            "$ref": "User"
        },
        "token": {
            "description": "JWT token containing claims for exp, roles, and permissions (not part of request, only response)",
            "type": "string"
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
  "email": "jdoe@somewhere.com",
  "user": {
    "id": 1,
    "email": "jdoe@anywhere.com",
    "firstName": "John",
    "lastName": "Doe",
    "profileImageUrl": "assets/temp/John_Smith.jpg",

      "administrator",
      "customer"
    ]
  },
  "token": "eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJJc3N1ZXIiOiJodHRwOi8vd3d3Lnd5bnlhcmRncm91cC5jb20iLCJBdWRpZW5jZSI6IkFDQSIsIlByaW5jaXBhbCI6eyJTZXNzaW9uSWQiOiI3ZDZjN2ZjMC1lNzkzLTQyNjMtOTQ3OC01MmQzMmQyYzYzNjEiLCJVc2VyS2V5IjoiNCIsIlVzZXJOYW1lIjoia2NsaWZmZSIsIkNsYWltcyI6WyJBZG1pbiJdLCJMb2NhbGUiOiJlbi1OWiIsIlNlc3Npb25UaW1lT3V0IjoiXC9EYXRlKDE0NTA3OTQ1OTczNjIpXC8iLCJJc3N1ZWRUbyI6bnVsbCwiSWRlbnRpdHkiOnsiTmFtZSI6ImtjbGlmZmUiLCJBdXRoZW50aWNhdGlvblR5cGUiOiJXeW55YXJkIiwiSXNBdXRoZW50aWNhdGVkIjp0cnVlfX0sIkV4cGlyeSI6IlwvRGF0ZSgxKVwvIn0.0GZlnA-mdDQqSfSKvBlWsUehtVCRkNK8DA9siyeVLQ0"

/surveys

Management of survey resources

/surveys post get

post

Add a new survey to the collection

get

Get a list of survey

post /surveys

Add a new survey to the collection

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Survey",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["surveyId"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "surveyId": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "sections": {
            "description": "Question sections that comprise the survey",
            "$ref": "SectionCollection"
        }
    }
}

Example:

{
    "surveyId": "1",
    "sections": [
        {
            "sectionId": "1",
            "title": "Risk Appetite and Tolerance",
            "subsections": [
                {
                    "subsectionId": "1",
                    "title": "Are risks considered as a component of organization strategy?",
                    "questions": [
                        {
                            "questionId": "1",
                            "text": "Does the organization formally consider risk in strategic planning?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"]
                        },
                        {
                            "questionId": "2",
                            "text": "Does the organization consider risk when setting new business strategies?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"],
                            "dependentIds": ["1"]
                        },
                        {
                            "questionId": "3",
                            "text": "Are risks formally documented?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"],
                            "dependentIds": ["2"]
                        },
                        {
                            "questionId": "4",
                            "text": "Are risk management activities integrated within organization business strategy development and governance?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"],
                            "dependentIds": ["3"]
                        },
                        {
                            "questionId": "5",
                            "text": "Does the organization utilize the ERM Program to integrate risk within strategic planning development and business forecasting?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"],
                            "dependentIds": ["4"]
                        },
                        {
                            "questionId": "6",
                            "text": "Is risk scenario analysis used for business planning and quantitative analysis used to understand capital allocation and funding levels?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"],
                            "dependentIds": ["4"]
                        }
                    ],
                    "scoreLevels": [
                        {
                            "description": "Organization does not formally consider risk in strategic planning.",
                            "requiredQuestionIds": ["1"]
                        },
                        {
                            "description": "Organization considers risk when setting new business strategies. Risk that impacts the execution of strategy may be considered but are not formally documented.",
                            "requiredQuestionIds": ["1", "2"]
                        },
                        {
                            "description": "Consideration of risk is a key aspect of organization's strategic planning. Risks are formally documented.",
                            "requiredQuestionIds": ["1", "2", "3"]
                        },
                        {
                            "description": "Risk management activities are integrated within organization business strategy development and governance.",
                            "requiredQuestionIds": ["1", "2", "3", "4"]
                        },
                        {
                            "description": "Organization utilizes the ERM Program to integrate risk within strategic planning development and business forecasting. Risk scenario analysis is used for business planning and quantitative analysis is used to understand capital allocation and funding levels.",
                            "requiredQuestionIds": ["1", "2", "3", "4", "5", "6"]
                        }                        
                    ]
                },
                {
                    "subsectionId": "2",
                    "title": "Is the risk appetite of organization clearly defined and understood?",
                    "questions": [
                        {
                            "questionId": "7",
                            "text": "Does the organization have a meaningful definition or understanding of the overall corporate risk appetite?",
                            "responses": ["Yes", "No"]
                        },

HTTP status code 201

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Survey",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["surveyId"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "surveyId": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "sections": {
            "description": "Question sections that comprise the survey",
            "$ref": "SectionCollection"
        }
    }
}

This is a mock service that has not yet been implemented

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 409

Unable to process request to do conflict in state of object. Any specific details included in body.

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those

get /surveys

Get a list of survey

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/SurveyCollection",
    "type": "array",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "items": {
        "$ref": "Survey"
    }
}

Example:

[
    {
        "surveyId": "123"
    },
    {
        "surveyId": "456"
    }
]

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 404

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those

/surveys/{surveyId} put delete get

Management of a survey resource

put

Update a specific survey

delete

Deletes a specific survey

get

Get a specific survey

put /surveys/{surveyId}

Update a specific survey

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • surveyId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Survey",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["surveyId"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "surveyId": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "sections": {
            "description": "Question sections that comprise the survey",
            "$ref": "SectionCollection"
        }
    }
}

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Survey",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["surveyId"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "surveyId": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "sections": {
            "description": "Question sections that comprise the survey",
            "$ref": "SectionCollection"
        }
    }
}

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 404

Unable to find survey by id.

HTTP status code 409

Unable to process request to do conflict in state of object. Any specific details included in body.

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those

delete /surveys/{surveyId}

Deletes a specific survey

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • surveyId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

HTTP status code 204

Successfully deleted the survey

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 404

Unable to find survey by id.

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those

get /surveys/{surveyId}

Get a specific survey

Secured by JWT
  • Request
  • Response
  • Security

URI Parameters

  • surveyId: required (string)

Headers

  • X-AUTH-TOKEN: (string)

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
    "id": "http://types/Survey",
    "type": "object",
    "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema",
    "required": ["surveyId"],
    "additionalProperties": false,
    "properties": {
        "surveyId": {
            "description": "The identifier of the object",
            "type": "string"
        },
        "sections": {
            "description": "Question sections that comprise the survey",
            "$ref": "SectionCollection"
        }
    }
}

HTTP status code 401

Authentication token is invalid or has expired. Client should display a message to the user and return them user to the login screen.

HTTP status code 403

Authentication token is valid, but client does not have access to perform this action.

HTTP status code 404

Unable to find survey by id.

Secured by JWT

Headers

  • Authorization: required ()

    JWT token containing claims for 'exp' (expiration), 'roles', and 'permissions'. TODO: define the format for each of those
